         <div class="js-text-shrink" data-collection-id="54fa26f0e4b0e615760a28df" data-edit-main-image="Page Banner" id="page-title-wrapper">
          <h1 class="page-title" id="page-title">
           HOME PLATE
          </h1>
          <div class="page-description" id="page-description">
           <p>
            <span style="font-size:small">
             The Canadian Baseball Network ( CBN ) promotes
            </span>
            <strong>
             Canadian baseball
            </strong>
            <span style="font-size:small">
             players and teams from coast to coast. The Canadian Baseball Network features a
             <strong>
              draft list,
             </strong>
             ranking of the top
            </span>
            Canadian
            <strong>
            </strong>
            baseball
            <span style="font-size:small">
             <strong>
              prospects
             </strong>
             and featured articles.
            </span>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>

         <div class="site-info">
          <h3 class="site-title">
           Canadian Baseball Network
          </h3>
          <div class="site-description">
           <p>
            <span style="font-size:small">
             The Canadian Baseball Network ( CBN ) promotes
            </span>
            <strong>
             Canadian Baseball
            </strong>
            <span style="font-size:small">
             players and teams from coast to coast. The Canadian Baseball Network features our D
             <strong>
              raft List,
             </strong>
             ranking the top
            </span>
            Canadian
            <strong>
            </strong>
            baseball
            <span style="font-size:small">
             <strong>
              prospects
             </strong>
             and featured articles.
            </span>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>

            <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_62_1505482218536_55396">
             <div class="sqs-block-content">
              <h2 class="text-align-center">
               Tip of the Month: brought to you  by
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="sqs-block image-block sqs-block-image" data-block-type="5" id="block-yui_3_17_2_17_1507318310315_48570">
             <div class="sqs-block-content">
              <div class="image-block-outer-wrapper layout-caption-hidden design-layout-inline">
               <div class="intrinsic" style="max-width:807.0px;">
                <a href="/cbn-tip-of-the-month" target="_blank">
